namespace = apsr_terminal

# Занятые номера:
# 1 - скрытый - присвоение кодов для терминала
# 2 - скрытый - проверка введенного кода в терминале
# 101-165 - сообщения при подборе правильного сгенерированного кода
# 198 - сообщение про повторном наборе кода + блокировка
# 199 - не подошел ни один из кодов
# 201-265 - сообщения при изучении места с наградой от сгенерированного кода (первое изучение = 100% от награды)
# 301-365 - сообщения при изучении места с наградой от сгенерированного кода (последующие изучения = 10% от награды)
# 80001-80002 - кураторы предлагают приобрести код
# 81001-81004 - угасшие дают координаты/код
# 82001-82004 - найден код при расчистке тайлблокера
# 90000 - сообщение при активации кода 0000
# 90001-90007 - сообщения при изучении аномалии
# 90025 - сообщение при активации кода 0025 (генерация кодов)
# 90076 - сообщение при активации кода 0076 (просмотр кодов)
# 90451 - награда за код 0451
# 92012 - награда за код 2012
# 96110-96180 - раскопки Кукурузы
# 96201-96202 - дополнительные события кода 62
# 96301 - дополнительные события кода 63
# 96401 - дополнительные события кода 64
# 96501-96522 - дополнительные события кода 65
# 99029 - награда за код 9029
# 99900 - присвоение меток системам - скрипт движения флотов из засад
# 99996 - использование реликвии для ИИ
# 99998 - если нашел ВСЕ коды
# 99999 - окно терминала

# 0076 - просмотреть список кодов - apsr_terminal.90076





country_event = {
	id = apsr_terminal.99999
	title = "apsr_terminal_open"
	desc = "OK"
	diplomatic = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	custom_gui = apsr_terminal_overview
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

### СООБЩЕНИЕ ПРИ ПРАВИЛЬНОМ КОДЕ (ГЕНЕРИРУЕМЫЕ)


# 01
country_event = {
	id = apsr_terminal.101
	title = apsr_terminal.101.title
	desc = apsr_terminal.101.desc
	picture = GFX_apsr_terminal_reward
	show_sound = relic_activation_isolated_contingency_core

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { exists = event_target:apsr_terminal_site_01 }
			}
			random_system = {
				limit = {
					any_system_planet = {
						is_star = no
						is_colony = no
						is_capital = no
						habitable_structure = no
						is_asteroid = no
						NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_gas_giant }
					}
				}
				random_system_planet = {
					limit = {
						is_star = no
						is_colony = no
						is_capital = no
						habitable_structure = no
						is_asteroid = no
						NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_gas_giant }
					}
					save_global_event_target_as = apsr_terminal_site_01
				}		
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = apsr_terminal.101.button
		custom_tooltip = apsr_terminal.101.button.tooltip
		enable_special_project = {
			name = "apsr_terminal_site_01"
			location = event_target:apsr_terminal_site_01
			owner = root
		}
		add_event_chain_counter = { 
			event_chain = "apsr_terminal_coordinates_log" 
			counter = "apsr_terminal_coordinates_num" 
			amount = 1 
		}
	}
}

			limit = {
				NOT = { exists = event_target:apsr_terminal_site_59 }
			}
			random_system = {
				limit = {
					any_system_planet = {
						is_star = no
						is_colony = no
						is_capital = no
						habitable_structure = no
						is_asteroid = no
						NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_gas_giant }
					}
				}
				random_system_planet = {
					limit = {
						is_star = no
						is_colony = no
						is_capital = no
						habitable_structure = no
						is_asteroid = no
						NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_gas_giant }
					}
					save_global_event_target_as = apsr_terminal_site_59
				}		
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = apsr_terminal.159.button
		custom_tooltip = apsr_terminal.159.button.tooltip
		enable_special_project = {
			name = "apsr_terminal_site_59"
			location = event_target:apsr_terminal_site_59
			owner = root
		}
		add_event_chain_counter = { 
			event_chain = "apsr_terminal_coordinates_log" 
			counter = "apsr_terminal_coordinates_num" 
			amount = 1 
		}
	}
}

# 61
country_event = {
	id = apsr_terminal.161
	title = apsr_terminal.161.title
	desc = apsr_terminal.161.desc
	picture = GFX_apsr_terminal_reward
	show_sound = relic_activation_isolated_contingency_core

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { exists = event_target:apsr_terminal_site_61 }
			}
			random_system = {
				limit = {
					exists = owner
					owner = { is_same_value = root }
					any_system_planet = {
						is_star = no
						is_capital = no
						habitable_structure = no
						is_asteroid = no
						NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_gas_giant }
						NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_city }
					}
				}
				random_system_planet = {
					limit = {
						is_star = no
						is_capital = no
						habitable_structure = no
						is_asteroid = no
						NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_gas_giant }
						NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_city }
					}
					save_global_event_target_as = apsr_terminal_site_61
				}		
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = apsr_terminal.161.button1
		custom_tooltip = apsr_terminal.161.button1.tooltip
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_ethic = ethic_authoritarian
						has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_authoritarian
					}
				}
			}
		}
		enable_special_project = {
			name = "apsr_terminal_site_61"
			location = event_target:apsr_terminal_site_61
			owner = root
		}
		add_event_chain_counter = { 
			event_chain = "apsr_terminal_coordinates_log" 
			counter = "apsr_terminal_coordinates_num" 
			amount = 1 
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = apsr_terminal.161.button2

		trigger = {
			owner = {
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_authoritarian

				}
			}
		}
		enable_special_project = {
			name = "apsr_terminal_site_61"
			location = event_target:apsr_terminal_site_61
			owner = root
		}
		add_event_chain_counter = { 
			event_chain = "apsr_terminal_coordinates_log" 
			counter = "apsr_terminal_coordinates_num" 
			amount = 1 
		}
	}

# 51
country_event = {
	id = apsr_terminal.251
	title = apsr_terminal.251.title
	desc = apsr_terminal.251.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_unidentified_monster
	show_sound = event_ai_started

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		event_target:apsr_terminal_site_51 = {
			solar_system = {
				random_neighbor_system = {
					random_system_planet = {
						save_global_event_target_as = apsr_terminal_fleet_51_waypoint
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { exists = event_target:apsr_terminal_unknown_country } }
			create_country = {
				name = "NAME_apsr_terminal_unknown_country"
				type = apsr_terminal_unknown_country
				flag = {
					icon = {
						category = "special"
						file = "unknown.dds"
					}
					background= {
						category = "backgrounds"
						file = "00_solid.dds"
					}
					colors={
						"black"
						"black"
						"null"
						"null"
					}
				}
				effect = {
					set_name = "apsr_terminal_unknown_country_name"
					save_global_event_target_as = apsr_terminal_unknown_country
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = "apsr_terminal_unknown_country_modifier"
						days = -1
					}
					every_playable_country = {
						establish_communications_no_message = event_target:apsr_terminal_unknown_country
					}
				}
			}
		}
		create_fleet = {
			name = "NAME_apsr_terminal_unknown_country_fleet_1"
			settings = {
				spawn_debris = no
				is_boss = yes
			}
			effect = {
				set_owner = event_target:apsr_terminal_unknown_country
				while = {
					count = 16
					create_ship = {
						name = ""
						design = "NAME_Bemat_corvette_01"
						graphical_culture = "pirate_01"
					}
				}
				while = {
					count = 7
					create_ship = {
						name = ""
						design = "NAME_Bemat_destroyer_01"
						graphical_culture = "pirate_01"
					}
				}
				while = {
					count = 5
					create_ship = {
						name = ""
						design = "NAME_Bemat_destroyer_02"
						graphical_culture = "pirate_01"
					}
				}
				while = {
					count = 2
					create_ship = {
						name = ""
						design = "NAME_Bemat_cruiser_01"
						graphical_culture = "pirate_01"
					}
				}
				while = {
					count = 3
					create_ship = {
						name = ""
						design = "NAME_Bemat_cruiser_02"
						graphical_culture = "pirate_01"
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						mid_game_years_passed >= 0
					}
					while = {
						count = 16
						create_ship = {
							name = ""
							design = "NAME_Bemat_corvette_01"
							graphical_culture = "pirate_01"
						}
					}
					while = {
						count = 7
						create_ship = {
							name = ""
							design = "NAME_Bemat_destroyer_01"
							graphical_culture = "pirate_01"
						}
					}
					while = {
						count = 5
						create_ship = {
							name = ""
							design = "NAME_Bemat_destroyer_02"
							graphical_culture = "pirate_01"
						}
					}
					while = {
						count = 2
						create_ship = {
							name = ""
							design = "NAME_Bemat_cruiser_01"
							graphical_culture = "pirate_01"
						}
					}
					while = {
						count = 3
						create_ship = {
							name = ""
							design = "NAME_Bemat_cruiser_02"
							graphical_culture = "pirate_01"
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						end_game_years_passed >= 0
					}
					while = {
						count = 16
						create_ship = {
							name = ""
							design = "NAME_Bemat_corvette_01"
							graphical_culture = "pirate_01"
						}
					}
					while = {
						count = 7
						create_ship = {
							name = ""
							design = "NAME_Bemat_destroyer_01"
							graphical_culture = "pirate_01"
						}
					}
					while = {
						count = 5
						create_ship = {
							name = ""
							design = "NAME_Bemat_destroyer_02"
							graphical_culture = "pirate_01"
						}
					}
					while = {
						count = 2
						create_ship = {
							name = ""
							design = "NAME_Bemat_cruiser_01"
							graphical_culture = "pirate_01"
						}
					}
					while = {
						count = 3
						create_ship = {
							name = ""
							design = "NAME_Bemat_cruiser_02"
							graphical_culture = "pirate_01"
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						end_game_years_passed >= 100
					}
					while = {
						count = 3
						create_ship = {
							name = ""
							design = "NAME_Bemat_corvette_01"
							graphical_culture = "pirate_01"
						}
					}
					while = {
						count = 5
						create_ship = {
							name = ""
							design = "NAME_Bemat_destroyer_01"
							graphical_culture = "pirate_01"
						}
					}
					while = {
						count = 5
						create_ship = {
							name = ""
							design = "NAME_Bemat_destroyer_02"
							graphical_culture = "pirate_01"
						}
					}
					while = {
						count = 6
						create_ship = {
							name = ""
							design = "NAME_Bemat_cruiser_01"
							graphical_culture = "pirate_01"
						}
					}
					while = {
						count = 6
						create_ship = {
							name = ""
							design = "NAME_Bemat_cruiser_02"
							graphical_culture = "pirate_01"
						}
					}
				}
				set_name = "apsr_terminal_unknown_country_name"
				set_fleet_flag = apsr_terminal_unknown_fleet
				set_location = event_target:apsr_terminal_site_51
				set_formation_scale = 3
				set_fleet_stance = aggressive
				set_aggro_range_measure_from = self
				set_aggro_range = 50
				queue_actions = {
					repeat = {
						find_closest_system = {
							trigger = {
								id = apsr_terminal_code_51.waypoint1
								NOR = {
									any_fleet_in_system = {
										has_fleet_flag = apsr_terminal_unknown_fleet
									}
									has_star_flag = apsr_terminal_unknown_fleet_visited
								}
							}
							found_system = {
								move_to = this
								find_closest_planet = {
									trigger = {
										id = apsr_terminal_code_51.waypoint2
										is_star = yes
									}
									found_planet = {
										move_to = this
										wait = {
											duration = 120
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = apsr_terminal.251.button
		custom_tooltip = apsr_terminal.251.button.tooltip
	}
}

									}
									has_star_flag = apsr_terminal_unknown_fleet_visited
								}
							}
							found_system = {
								move_to = this
								find_closest_planet = {
									trigger = {
										id = apsr_terminal_code_52.waypoint2
										is_star = yes
									}
									found_planet = {
										move_to = this
										wait = {
											duration = 120
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = apsr_terminal.252.button
		custom_tooltip = apsr_terminal.252.button.tooltip
	}
}

# 53
country_event = {
	id = apsr_terminal.253
	title = apsr_terminal.253.title
	desc = apsr_terminal.253.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_unidentified_monster
	show_sound = event_ai_started

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		event_target:apsr_terminal_site_53 = {
			solar_system = {
				random_neighbor_system = {
					random_system_planet = {
						save_global_event_target_as = apsr_terminal_fleet_53_waypoint
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { exists = event_target:apsr_terminal_unknown_country } }
			create_country = {
				name = "NAME_apsr_terminal_unknown_country"
				type = apsr_terminal_unknown_country
				flag = {
					icon = {
						category = "special"
						file = "unknown.dds"
					}
					background= {
						category = "backgrounds"
						file = "00_solid.dds"
					}
					colors={
						"black"
						"black"
						"null"
						"null"
					}
				}
				effect = {
					set_name = "apsr_terminal_unknown_country_name"
					save_global_event_target_as = apsr_terminal_unknown_country
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = "apsr_terminal_unknown_country_modifier"
						days = -1
					}
					every_playable_country = {
						establish_communications_no_message = event_target:apsr_terminal_unknown_country
					}
				}
			}
		}
		create_fleet = {
			name = "NAME_apsr_terminal_unknown_country_fleet_3"
			settings = {
				spawn_debris = no
				is_boss = yes
			}
			effect = {
				set_owner = event_target:apsr_terminal_unknown_country
				while = {
					count = 4
					create_ship = {
						name = ""
						design = "NAME_Nanite_Interdictor"
						graphical_culture = "pirate_01"
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						mid_game_years_passed >= 0
					}
					while = {
						count = 4
						create_ship = {
							name = ""
							design = "NAME_Nanite_Interdictor"
							graphical_culture = "pirate_01"
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						end_game_years_passed >= 0
					}
					while = {
						count = 1
						create_ship = {
							name = ""
							design = "NAME_Nanite_Mothership"
							graphical_culture = "pirate_01"
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						end_game_years_passed >= 100
					}
					while = {
						count = 2
						create_ship = {
							name = ""
							design = "NAME_Nanite_Mothership"
							graphical_culture = "pirate_01"
						}
					}
				}
				set_name = "apsr_terminal_unknown_country_name"
				set_fleet_flag = apsr_terminal_unknown_fleet
				set_location = event_target:apsr_terminal_site_53
				set_formation_scale = 3
				set_fleet_stance = aggressive
				set_aggro_range_measure_from = self
				set_aggro_range = 50
				queue_actions = {
					repeat = {
						find_closest_system = {
							trigger = {
								id = apsr_terminal_code_53.waypoint1
								NOR = {
									any_fleet_in_system = {
										has_fleet_flag = apsr_terminal_unknown_fleet
									}
									has_star_flag = apsr_terminal_unknown_fleet_visited
								}
							}
							found_system = {
								move_to = this
								find_closest_planet = {
									trigger = {
										id = apsr_terminal_code_53.waypoint2
										is_star = yes
									}
									found_planet = {
										move_to = this
										wait = {
											duration = 120
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = apsr_terminal.253.button
		custom_tooltip = apsr_terminal.253.button.tooltip
	}
}

									}
									has_star_flag = apsr_terminal_unknown_fleet_visited
								}
							}

									}

# 61
country_event = {
	id = apsr_terminal.361
	title = apsr_terminal.361.title
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = apsr_terminal_site_61_complete
			}
		}
		text = "apsr_terminal.361.desc1"
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = apsr_terminal_site_61_complete
		}
		text = "apsr_terminal.361.desc2"
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_ship_in_orbit_3
	show_sound = event_mystic_reveal_light

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = apsr_terminal.361.button1
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = apsr_terminal_site_61_complete
				}
				NOR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_xenophobe
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe
					has_ethic = ethic_militarist
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_militarist
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = apsr_terminal.361.button2
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = apsr_terminal_site_61_complete
				}
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_xenophobe
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe
					has_ethic = ethic_militarist
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_militarist
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = apsr_terminal.361.button3
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = apsr_terminal_site_61_complete
		}
	}
}

# 0025 - пересоздание кодов
country_event = {
	id = apsr_terminal.90025
	title = apsr_terminal.90025.title
	desc = apsr_terminal.90025.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_apsr_logo

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = apsr_terminal.90025.button1
		custom_tooltip = apsr_terminal.90025.button1.tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = no
				}
				country_event = { id = apsr_terminal.1 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = apsr_terminal.90025.button2
	}
}

# 0076 - просмотр кодов
country_event = {
	id = apsr_terminal.90076
	title = apsr_terminal.90076.title
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = apsr_terminal_devactive
			}
		}
		text = "apsr_terminal.90076.desc0"
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = apsr_terminal_devactive
		}
		text = "apsr_terminal.90076.desc"
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_apsr_logo

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = apsr_terminal.90076.button
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = apsr_terminal_devactive
					}
				}
				set_timed_country_flag = { flag = apsr_terminal_devactive days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
}

### СООБЩЕНИЕ ПРИ НЕПРАВИЛЬНОМ КОДЕ

country_event = {
	id = apsr_terminal.199
	title = apsr_terminal.199.title
	desc = apsr_terminal.199.desc
	picture = GFX_apsr_terminal_block
	show_sound = event_ai_started

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		random_list = {
			40 = {
				set_timed_country_flag = {
					flag = apsr_terminal_block_time
					days = 1000
				}
			}
			20 = {
				set_timed_country_flag = {
					flag = apsr_terminal_block_time
					days = 1250
				}
			}
			20 = {
				set_timed_country_flag = {
					flag = apsr_terminal_block_time
					days = 1500
				}
			}
			10 = {
				set_timed_country_flag = {
					flag = apsr_terminal_block_time
					days = 1750
				}
			}
			10 = {
				set_timed_country_flag = {
					flag = apsr_terminal_block_time
					days = 2000
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = apsr_terminal.199.button
		custom_tooltip = apsr_terminal.199.button.tooltip
	}
}

### СООБЩЕНИЕ ПРИ ИЗУЧЕНИИ АНОМАЛИИ

# Получение Терминала
ship_event = {
	id = apsr_terminal.90001
	title = "apsr_terminal.90001.title"
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						apsr_terminal_has_any_code_info = yes
					}
					NOT = {
						has_relic = relic_apsr_terminal
					}
				}
			}
		}
		text = "apsr_terminal.90001.desc1"
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				AND = {
					apsr_terminal_has_any_code_info = yes
					NOT = {
						has_relic = relic_apsr_terminal
					}
				}
			}
		}
		text = "apsr_terminal.90001.desc2"
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				has_relic = relic_apsr_terminal
			}
		}
		text = "apsr_terminal.90001.desc3"
	}
	picture = GFX_apsr_terminal_anomaly
	show_sound = event_mystic_reveal
	location = FROM
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = apsr_terminal.90001.button1
		custom_tooltip = apsr_terminal.90001.button1.tooltip
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						apsr_terminal_has_any_code_info = yes
					}
					NOT = {
						has_relic = relic_apsr_terminal
					}
				}
			}
		}
		owner = {
			add_relic = relic_apsr_terminal
			set_country_flag = apsr_player_have_terminal
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = apsr_terminal.90001.button2
		custom_tooltip = apsr_terminal.90001.button2.tooltip
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				AND = {
					apsr_terminal_has_any_code_info = yes
					NOT = {
						has_relic = relic_apsr_terminal
					}
				}
			}
		}
		owner = {
			add_relic = relic_apsr_terminal
			set_country_flag = apsr_player_have_terminal
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = apsr_terminal.90001.button3
		custom_tooltip = apsr_terminal.90001.button3.tooltip
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				has_relic = relic_apsr_terminal
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			owner = {
				apsr_terminal_reward_code_level_5 = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

# 99900 - присвоение меток системам - скрипт движения флотов из засад
fleet_event = {
	id = apsr_terminal.99900
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = { has_fleet_flag = apsr_terminal_unknown_fleet }

	immediate = {
		random_list = {
			20 = {
				solar_system = {
					set_timed_star_flag = {
						flag = apsr_terminal_unknown_fleet_visited
						days = 700
					}
				}
			}
			20 = {
				solar_system = {
					set_timed_star_flag = {
						flag = apsr_terminal_unknown_fleet_visited
						days = 1000
					}
				}
			}
			20 = {
				solar_system = {

# Кураторы предлагают код
country_event = {
	id = apsr_terminal.80002
	title = apsr_terminal.80002.name
	desc = apsr_terminal.80002.desc

	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	custom_gui = "enclave_curator_window"

	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = event_target:curator_enclave_country
		room = enclave_curator_room
	}
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = attacked_curators }
		exists = event_target:curator_enclave_country
		has_modifier = curator_insight
		has_relic = relic_apsr_terminal
	}

	immediate = {
		set_timed_country_flag = { flag = apsr_terminal_code_from_curators days = 3600 }
	}

	# 1
	option = {
		name = apsr_terminal.80002.button1
		custom_tooltip = apsr_terminal.80002.button1.tooltip
		response_text = apsr_terminal.80002.button.reply
		custom_gui = "enclave_curator_option"
		allow = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= 5000 }
			hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = attacked_curators }
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = apsr_terminal_code_from_curators_lvl_1
		}
		add_resource = { energy = -5000 }
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				80 = {
					apsr_terminal_reward_code_level_1 = yes
				}
				10 = {
					apsr_terminal_reward_code_level_2 = yes
				}
				6 = {
					apsr_terminal_reward_code_level_3 = yes
				}
				3 = {
					apsr_terminal_reward_code_level_4 = yes
				}
				1 = {
					apsr_terminal_reward_code_level_5 = yes
				}
			}
			remove_country_flag = apsr_terminal_code_from_curators_lvl_1
			remove_country_flag = apsr_terminal_code_from_curators_lvl_2
			remove_country_flag = apsr_terminal_code_from_curators_lvl_3
			remove_country_flag = apsr_terminal_code_from_curators_lvl_4
			remove_country_flag = apsr_terminal_code_from_curators_lvl_5
		}
	}

	# 2
	option = {
		name = apsr_terminal.80002.button2
		custom_tooltip = apsr_terminal.80002.button2.tooltip
		response_text = apsr_terminal.80002.button.reply
		custom_gui = "enclave_curator_option"
		allow = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= 10000 }
			hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = attacked_curators }
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = apsr_terminal_code_from_curators_lvl_2
		}
		add_resource = { energy = -10000 }
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				7 = {
					apsr_terminal_reward_code_level_1 = yes
				}
				80 = {
					apsr_terminal_reward_code_level_2 = yes
				}
				8 = {
					apsr_terminal_reward_code_level_3 = yes
				}
				4 = {
					apsr_terminal_reward_code_level_4 = yes
				}
				1 = {
					apsr_terminal_reward_code_level_5 = yes
				}
			}
			remove_country_flag = apsr_terminal_code_from_curators_lvl_1
			remove_country_flag = apsr_terminal_code_from_curators_lvl_2
			remove_country_flag = apsr_terminal_code_from_curators_lvl_3
			remove_country_flag = apsr_terminal_code_from_curators_lvl_4
			remove_country_flag = apsr_terminal_code_from_curators_lvl_5
		}
	}

	# 3
	option = {
		name = apsr_terminal.80002.button3
		custom_tooltip = apsr_terminal.80002.button3.tooltip
		response_text = apsr_terminal.80002.button.reply
		custom_gui = "enclave_curator_option"
		allow = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= 15000 }

			}
		}

	option = { # отказ

fleet_event = {
	id = apsr_terminal.96110
	title = apsr_terminal.96110.title
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				is_gestalt = no
			}
		}
		text = "apsr_terminal.96110.desc1"
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				is_gestalt = yes
			}
		}
		text = "apsr_terminal.96110.desc2"
	}
	picture = GFX_apsr_dungeon
	show_sound = event_dig_site
	location = from

	archaeology = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		from = { set_site_progress_locked = yes }
		leader = {
			save_event_target_as = apsr_terminal_site_61_leader
		}
	}

	after = { 
		from = { set_site_progress_locked = no } 
	}

	option = {
		name = apsr_terminal.96110.button1
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				is_gestalt = no
			}
		}
		owner = {
			add_resource = { consumer_goods = -10 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					fleet_event = { id = apsr_terminal.96121 days = 180}
				}
				50 = {
					fleet_event = { id = apsr_terminal.96122 days = 180}
				}
			}
			owner = {
				set_country_flag = apsr_terminal_site_61_stage_2_events_unlock
			}
		}
	}

# Stage 7 - event 6/12
fleet_event = {
	id = apsr_terminal.96176
	title = apsr_terminal.96176.title
	desc = apsr_terminal.96176.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_fallen_empire_awakes
	show_sound = event_air_raid_siren_03
	location = from

	archaeology = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		owner = {
			has_country_flag = apsr_terminal_site_61_stage_7_events_unlock
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		fromfrom = { set_site_progress_locked = yes }
		leader = {
			save_event_target_as = apsr_terminal_site_61_leader
		}
	}

	after = { 
		fromfrom = { set_site_progress_locked = no } 
	}

	option = {
		name = apsr_terminal.96176.button
		fromfrom = { add_stage_clues = -3 }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { exists = event_target:apsr_terminal_unknown_country } }
				create_country = {
					name = "NAME_apsr_terminal_unknown_country"
					type = apsr_terminal_unknown_country
					flag = {
						icon = {
							category = "special"
							file = "unknown.dds"
						}
						background= {
							category = "backgrounds"
							file = "00_solid.dds"
						}
						colors={
							"black"
							"black"
							"null"
							"null"
						}
					}
					effect = {
						set_name = "apsr_terminal_unknown_country_name"
					}
				}
				last_created_country = {
					establish_communications_no_message = root
					save_global_event_target_as = apsr_terminal_unknown_country
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = "apsr_terminal_unknown_country_modifier"
						days = -1
					}
				}
			}
			create_fleet = {
				name = "NAME_apsr_terminal_unknown_country_fleet_61"
				settings = {
					spawn_debris = no
					is_boss = yes
				}
				effect = {
					set_owner = event_target:apsr_terminal_unknown_country
					while = {
						count = 1
						create_ship = {
							name = ""
							design = "NAME_Alpha"
							graphical_culture = "fallen_empire_01"
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							mid_game_years_passed >= 0
						}
						while = {
							count = 1
							create_ship = {
								name = ""
								design = "NAME_Alpha"
								graphical_culture = "fallen_empire_01"
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							end_game_years_passed >= 0
						}
						while = {
							count = 1
							create_ship = {
								name = ""
								design = "NAME_Alpha"
								graphical_culture = "fallen_empire_01"
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							end_game_years_passed >= 100
						}
						while = {
							count = 2
							create_ship = {
								name = ""
								design = "NAME_Alpha"
								graphical_culture = "fallen_empire_01"
							}
						}
					}
					set_name = "apsr_terminal_unknown_country_name"
					set_fleet_flag = apsr_terminal_unknown_fleet
					set_location = event_target:apsr_terminal_site_61
					set_formation_scale = 3
					set_fleet_stance = aggressive
					set_aggro_range_measure_from = self
					set_aggro_range = 500
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

fleet_event = {
	id = apsr_terminal.96178
	title = apsr_terminal.96178.title
	desc = apsr_terminal.96178.desc
	picture = GFX_apsr_terminal_rising_monster
	show_sound = event_air_raid_siren_03
	location = from

	archaeology = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		owner = {
			has_country_flag = apsr_terminal_site_61_stage_7_events_unlock
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		fromfrom = { set_site_progress_locked = yes }
		leader = {
			save_event_target_as = apsr_terminal_site_61_leader
		}
	}

	after = { 
		fromfrom = { set_site_progress_locked = no } 
	}

	option = {
		name = apsr_terminal.96178.button
		fromfrom = { add_stage_clues = -3 }
		event_target:apsr_terminal_site_61 = {
			add_planet_devastation = 10
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { exists = event_target:apsr_terminal_unknown_country } }
				create_country = {
					name = "NAME_apsr_terminal_unknown_country"
					type = apsr_terminal_unknown_country
					flag = {
						icon = {
							category = "special"
							file = "unknown.dds"
						}
						background= {
							category = "backgrounds"
							file = "00_solid.dds"
						}
						colors={
							"black"
							"black"
							"null"
							"null"
						}
					}
					effect = {
						set_name = "apsr_terminal_unknown_country_name"
					}
				}
				last_created_country = {
					establish_communications_no_message = root
					save_global_event_target_as = apsr_terminal_unknown_country
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = "apsr_terminal_unknown_country_modifier"
						days = -1
					}
				}
			}
			event_target:apsr_terminal_site_61 = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_colony = yes
					}
					create_army = {
						name = random
						owner = event_target:apsr_terminal_unknown_country
						type = "machine_assault_3"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			}
		}

	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				is_gestalt = yes
				NOT = {
					has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence
				}
			}
		}
		text = "apsr_terminal.96180.desc2"
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				is_gestalt = yes
				has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence
			}
		}
		text = "apsr_terminal.96180.desc3"
	}
	picture = GFX_apsr_terminal_corn
	show_sound = evn_lootbox_galatron_01
	location = from

	archaeology = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		from = { set_site_progress_locked = yes }
		leader = {
			save_event_target_as = apsr_terminal_site_61_leader
			exile_leader_as = apsr_terminal_site_61_leader
		}
		owner = {
			set_country_flag = apsr_player_complete_corn
		}		
	}

	after = { 
		from = { set_site_progress_locked = no } 
	}

	option = {
		name = apsr_terminal.96180.button
		owner = {
			add_resource = { food = 1 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			owner = {
				remove_country_flag = apsr_terminal_site_61_stage_8_events_unlock
			}
			event_target:apsr_terminal_site_61_leader = {
				kill_leader = { show_notification = no }
			}
		}
	}
}

# изучение спецпроекта 65b - провал
country_event = {
	id = apsr_terminal.96504
	title = apsr_terminal.96504.title
	desc = apsr_terminal.96504.desc
	picture = GFX_apsr_robots
	show_sound = event_robo

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = apsr_terminal_site_65_main_player
		event_target:apsr_terminal_site_65 = {
			solar_system = {
				random_neighbor_system = {
					random_system_planet = {
						save_global_event_target_as = apsr_terminal_fleet_65_waypoint
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { exists = event_target:apsr_terminal_unknown_country } }
			create_country = {
				name = "NAME_apsr_terminal_unknown_country"
				type = apsr_terminal_unknown_country
				flag = {
					icon = {
						category = "special"
						file = "unknown.dds"
					}
					background= {
						category = "backgrounds"
						file = "00_solid.dds"
					}
					colors={
						"black"
						"black"
						"null"
						"null"
					}
				}
				effect = {
					set_name = "apsr_terminal_unknown_country_name"
				}
			}
			last_created_country = {
				establish_communications_no_message = root
				save_global_event_target_as = apsr_terminal_unknown_country
				add_modifier = {
					modifier = "apsr_terminal_unknown_country_modifier"
					days = -1
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:apsr_terminal_unknown_country = {
			create_leader = {
				class = admiral
				species = event_target:apsr_terminal_unknown_country
				name = random
				skill = 5
				effect = {
					set_age = 5
				}
			}
		}
		create_fleet = {
			name = "NAME_apsr_terminal_unknown_country_fleet_65"
			settings = {
				spawn_debris = no
				#is_boss = yes
			}
			effect = {
				set_owner = event_target:apsr_terminal_unknown_country
				while = {
					count = 5
					create_ship = {
						name = random
						design = "NAME_Euthanizer"
						graphical_culture = "ai_01"
					}
				}
				while = {
					count = 10
					create_ship = {
						name = random
						design = "NAME_Sterilizer"
						graphical_culture = "ai_01"
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						mid_game_years_passed >= 0
					}
					while = {
						count = 10
						create_ship = {
							name = ""
							design = "NAME_Sterilizer"
							graphical_culture = "ai_01"
						}
					}
					while = {
						count = 5
						create_ship = {
							name = ""
							design = "NAME_Euthanizer"
							graphical_culture = "ai_01"
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						end_game_years_passed >= 0
					}
					while = {
						count = 10
						create_ship = {
							name = ""
							design = "NAME_Sterilizer"
							graphical_culture = "ai_01"
						}
					}
					while = {
						count = 5
						create_ship = {
							name = ""
							design = "NAME_Euthanizer"
							graphical_culture = "ai_01"
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						end_game_years_passed >= 100
					}
					while = {
						count = 10
						create_ship = {
							name = ""
							design = "NAME_Sterilizer"
							graphical_culture = "ai_01"
						}
					}
					while = {
						count = 5
						create_ship = {
							name = ""
							design = "NAME_Euthanizer"
							graphical_culture = "ai_01"
						}
					}
				}
				set_name = "apsr_terminal_unknown_country_name"
				assign_leader = last_created
				set_fleet_flag = apsr_terminal_unknown_fleet
				set_location = event_target:apsr_terminal_site_65
				set_formation_scale = 3
				set_fleet_stance = aggressive
				set_aggro_range_measure_from = self
				set_aggro_range = 50
				queue_actions = {
					repeat = {
						find_closest_system = {
							trigger = {
								id = apsr_terminal_code_65.waypoint1
								NOR = {
									any_fleet_in_system = {
										has_fleet_flag = apsr_terminal_unknown_fleet
									}
									has_star_flag = apsr_terminal_unknown_fleet_visited
								}
							}
							found_system = {
								move_to = this
								find_closest_planet = {
									trigger = {
										id = apsr_terminal_code_65.waypoint2
										is_star = yes
									}
									found_planet = {
										move_to = this
										wait = {
											duration = 120
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = apsr_terminal.96504.button
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOR = {
						is_machine_empire = yes
						has_technology = tech_synthetic_workers 
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = apsr_terminal.96511 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_machine_empire = yes
						has_technology = tech_synthetic_workers 
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = apsr_terminal.96512 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = apsr_terminal.96513.desc
	diplomatic_title = BLANK_STRING

	diplomatic = yes
	force_open = yes

	picture_event_data = {
		room = no_video_feed_room
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		FROM = {
			is_country_type = apsr_terminal_unknown_country
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = apsr_terminal_unknown_country_diplomacy_engaged }
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = apsr_terminal_unknown_country_diplomacy_engaged
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_country_flag = apsr_terminal_unknown_country_diplomacy_engaged
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = apsr_terminal.96513.button
	}
}

# Распределение подарков
country_event = {
	id = apsr_terminal.81002
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					any_country = {
						OR = {
							is_country_type = fallen_empire
							is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire 
						}
						has_communications = root
						NOT = { is_at_war_with = root }
						opinion = { who = root value > 99 }
					}
					root = {
						has_country_flag = apsr_terminal_code_from_fallen_type_1
						NOT ={
							has_relic = relic_apsr_terminal
						}
					}
				}
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = { 
					AND = {
						OR = {
							is_country_type = fallen_empire
							is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire 
						}
						has_communications = root
						NOT = { is_at_war_with = root }
						opinion = { who = root value > 99 }
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = apsr_terminal_gift_fallen_empire
			}
			random_system = {
				limit = {
					any_system_planet = {
						is_star = no
						is_colony = no
						is_capital = no
						habitable_structure = no
						is_asteroid = no
						NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_gas_giant }
					}
				}
				random_system_planet = {
					limit = {
						is_star = no
						is_colony = no
						is_capital = no
						habitable_structure = no
						is_asteroid = no
						NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_gas_giant }
					}
					save_event_target_as = apsr_terminal_site_relic
				}		
			}
			country_event = { id = apsr_terminal.81003 }
			remove_country_flag = apsr_terminal_code_from_fallen_type_1
			remove_country_flag = apsr_terminal_code_from_fallen_type_2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					any_country = {
						OR = {
							is_country_type = fallen_empire
							is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire 
						}
						has_communications = root
						NOT = { is_at_war_with = root }
						opinion = { who = root value > 99 }
					}
					root = {
						has_country_flag = apsr_terminal_code_from_fallen_type_2
					}
				}
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = { 
					AND = {
						OR = {
							is_country_type = fallen_empire
							is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire 
						}
						has_communications = root
						NOT = { is_at_war_with = root }
						opinion = { who = root value > 99 }
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = apsr_terminal_gift_fallen_empire
			}
			country_event = { id = apsr_terminal.81004 }
			remove_country_flag = apsr_terminal_code_from_fallen_type_1
			remove_country_flag = apsr_terminal_code_from_fallen_type_2
		}
	}
}

# Подарок - координаты реликвии
country_event = {
	id = apsr_terminal.81003
	title = "apsr_terminal.81003.title"
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			apsr_terminal_has_any_code_info = yes
		}
		text = "apsr_terminal.81003.desc1"
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				apsr_terminal_has_any_code_info = yes
			}
		}
		text = "apsr_terminal.81003.desc2"
	}

	diplomatic = yes
	
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = event_target:apsr_terminal_gift_fallen_empire
		planet_background = event_target:apsr_terminal_gift_fallen_empire
		graphical_culture = event_target:apsr_terminal_gift_fallen_empire
		city_level = event_target:apsr_terminal_gift_fallen_empire
		room = event_target:apsr_terminal_gift_fallen_empire.ruler
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = apsr_terminal.81003.button
		response_text = apsr_terminal.81003.button.reply
		enable_special_project = {
			name = "apsr_terminal_site_relic_fallen"
			location = event_target:apsr_terminal_site_relic
			owner = root
		}
	}
}

							is_deposit_type = d_segment_rubble_2 #Древние руины
						}

# сообщение - код
planet_event = {
    id = apsr_terminal.82002
	title = "apsr_terminal.82002.title"
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				has_planet_flag = apsr_terminal_blocker_code_unique
				owner = {
					NOT = {
						has_relic = relic_apsr_terminal
					}
				}
			}
		}
		text = apsr_terminal.82002.desc_unique
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				has_planet_flag = apsr_terminal_blocker_code_ancient
				owner = {
					NOT = {
						has_relic = relic_apsr_terminal
					}
				}
			}
		}
		text = apsr_terminal.82002.desc_ancient
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				has_planet_flag = apsr_terminal_blocker_code_ruined
				owner = {
					NOT = {
						has_relic = relic_apsr_terminal
					}
				}
			}
		}
		text = apsr_terminal.82002.desc_ruined
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_planet_flag = apsr_terminal_blocker_code_unique
						has_planet_flag = apsr_terminal_blocker_code_ancient
						has_planet_flag = apsr_terminal_blocker_code_ruined
					}
				}
				owner = {
					NOT = {
						has_relic = relic_apsr_terminal
					}
				}
			}
		}
		text = apsr_terminal.82002.desc_other
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				has_planet_flag = apsr_terminal_blocker_code_unique
				owner = {
					has_relic = relic_apsr_terminal
				}
			}
		}
		text = apsr_terminal.82002.desc_unique_r
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				has_planet_flag = apsr_terminal_blocker_code_ancient
				owner = {
					has_relic = relic_apsr_terminal

			}

    id = apsr_terminal.82003
	title = "apsr_terminal.82003.title"
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				NOT = {
					apsr_terminal_has_any_code_info = yes
				}
			}
		}
		text = apsr_terminal.82003.desc1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				apsr_terminal_has_any_code_info = yes
			}
		}
		text = apsr_terminal.82003.desc2
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_apsr15_construct
	show_sound = event_dig_site
	location = this

   	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = apsr_terminal.82003.button1
		custom_tooltip = apsr_terminal.82003.button1.tooltip
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						apsr_terminal_has_any_code_info = yes
					}
					NOT = {
						has_relic = relic_apsr_terminal
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			owner = {
				add_relic = relic_apsr_terminal
				set_country_flag = apsr_player_have_terminal
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = apsr_terminal.82003.button2
		custom_tooltip = apsr_terminal.82003.button2.tooltip
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				AND = {
					apsr_terminal_has_any_code_info = yes
					NOT = {
						has_relic = relic_apsr_terminal
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			owner = {
				add_relic = relic_apsr_terminal
				set_country_flag = apsr_player_have_terminal
			}
		}
	}
}
